Et por ceu sont li cautere plus legier, por ceu que tu en fais III a cop.	And because they are easier to cut, because you do three at a time.
de la dislocation de l’ajutoire	of the shoulder joint
Quant li chiés de l’ajutoire est desaloiez par cause de moistor, et on le remet a leu, et il n’i puet demorer ains revient adés et desalue par petit movement qui avient, si com nos avons esproveit, adonques covient il que tu ramoinnes la dislocation premierement.	When the head of the shoulder is dislocated due to moisture, and it is reset but cannot stay in place, repeatedly dislocating with slight movement as we have experienced, then you must first reset the dislocation.
Aprés soit sovinez li malaides sus son dos et sus son costeit;	Then stand the patient on his back and his side;
aprés lieve le keur qui est dedens le titillite as dois de ta main senestre;	After the knife is removed from the twitching, it is necessary to take it out with your left hand.
et se li jointure est desaluee dedens, si eschaufe le cautere qui a II ners douqueil ci est li forme:	and if the joint is dislocated within it, then cut the cautery with two needles in this form:
et cauterize lou keur tant qu’il le perce jusc’a costeit, et venrait li fugure dou cautere ensamble IIII cauteres;	and cauterize the wound so that it pierces just this side, and the figure of the cautery comes together with four cauteries;
et por ceu est faite cautere avec le cautere qui a III ners, por coi li figure de cauterization sunt sis cauteres;	and for this reason the cautery is made with the cautery that has three needles, because the figures of the cauterization are so four cauteries;
et sont li nerf selonc la subtiliteit d’une tente et c’est li forme dou cautere qui a III ners:	and they are the nerves according to the subtlety of a tent, and this is the form of the cautery that has three needles:
Et aucune fois est ajostez sus ce I nerf por coi il i a VIII cauteres.	And sometimes they press on this nerve because it has eight cauteries.
Aprés met sus le cautere porrelz broiez avec seil;	After placing the cautery on the flesh with thread;
aprés fai reposer le malaide, et ne soit meus li membres par lonc tens tant qu’il soit bien confortez.	After resting the patient, do not keep the limbs still for a long time until they are well comforted.
Et s’il est desaloiez desus, liquelz chose avient poc, adonques fait cautere sus l’epaisse dou cautere clavile, ou mout de cauteres en poignant.	And if the dislocation occurs above, then the case is poor, so make cauterization on the thick part with a cauterized needle or many cauterizations in a point.
Car li jointure est refermee, et est ostee li moistor et est sanez li malaides.	Because the joint is closed, and the moist part is healed, and the patient's sickness is alleviated.
Quant en l’estomac vienent froidures et mout de moistors tant qu’il l’estraient a sa complexion, et sont multipliet li catharre a lui, et es manieres de cures acostumees et il ne profite mie, adonc covient que li malaides soit sovinez sus son dos, et estende ses jambes et ses mains.	When colds and many moistors come to the stomach, and they extract them from his complexion, and multiply the catharres in him, and do all sorts of accustomed cures which he does not benefit from, then it is fitting that the sick person be laid on their back, and stretch out their legs and hands.
De ceu en aprés li fai III cauteres I desoz la cuillier dou pis per la quantiteit d’un doi, a tout le cautere clavile, et II cauteres defuers les II costez tant que li figure des cauteres soit a III angles, et ait teil espaice entre l’une et l’autre qu’elles ne soient jointes ensamble quant elles giteront porriture;	After that, you will perform the third cautery I under the earlobe with a spoon, of the amount of two, all over the cautery nail, and the second cautery on both sides so that the cautery figures are at three angles, and there is the same space between one and another as they will be joined together when they rot.
et soient li cautere si parfont qu’il porpreignent les II pars dou keur, et soit li figure des cauteres selonc ceste forme sens ajostement:	and when the cautery is applied in such a way that it inflames the two parts of the heart, and the figures of the cauteries are in this form next to each other:
Et se tu vues cauterize d’un grant cautere enmi l’estomac selonc ceste forme;	And if you see a large cautery being applied inside the stomach in this form;
et celui qui avra paour de cest cautere, cauterize en poignant et seigne sus l’estomac i. point selonc la quantiteit que tu vues d’enche;	And he who fears this cautery should be cauterized by pricking and pointing to the stomach at the same time as its quantity is seen.
puis le cauterize a tot le cautere qui est apelez «poins».	and then let him undergo the whole cautery, which is called "points".
Aprés le cure de la cure que nos avons eut devant, tant qu’il soit sanez.	After the treatment of the treatment we had previously, until it is healed.
Quant au foie vient dolor de froit et de moistor et de grosse ventositeit, tant qu’il est fuer mis de sa complexion natureil per les superfluitez;	when the liver comes with pain from frost and moisture and great ventosity, to the point that it is forced out of its natural state through superfluities;
et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne li profite mie, si covient que li malaides soit sovinez sus son haitereil;	and the patients are cured of what we have said in divisions, and it does them no good, unless they are covered over with their own bile.
et signe d’enche III cauteres selonc ceste forme et ceste figure et ceste quantiteit sus lou foie, defuer les ypocondres, lai ou li coutes de l’ome vient;	and a third point according to this form and shape and quantity on the liver, excluding the ypocondriac region, where the cost of the spleen comes.
et ait d’espaice entre chaicun cautere la groissece d’un doi;	And let there be space between each cautery the size of a doe;
et soient li cautere dou lonc dou cors, et ne presser mie mout ta main a tot le cautere;	and let the cauteries be long from head to body, and do not press too hard on your hand throughout the cautery;
et soit arse tant soulement li moitiez dou keur, et soit li malaides drois sus ses piez;	and let only the moist places be burned, and let the patient stand upright on his feet;
et s’il ne peut, si soit gisans, et estende ses jambes, et lieve ses brais;	and if he cannot, then let him sit, and stretch out his legs, and raise his arms;
et c’est li forme:	And this is the form:
Et se ta volentez est, si cauterize ces cauteres dou cutellaire, se tu es subtilz et saiges en l’art, et te warde que tu n’ardes mie tout le keur, car tu feroies sechier tout le cors;	And if you have your wish, then cauterize these cauteries on the cutellarie, being subtle and wise in this art, and beware lest you burn too much skin, for you will dry out the entire body;
et qu’il ne viegne jusc’a boueil, car li keurs est mout subtilz lai endroit, et lou saiches por voir.	and let him not come to boil, for the cuts are very subtle at that place, and one must know how to see.
Quant il a apostume au foie, et tu vues savoir s’il est en la char dou foie ou en la toile:	When there is an abscess on the liver, and you see whether it is in the flesh of the liver or in the net.
s’il est en la char, se sent li malaides dolor ne mie trop fort;	if it is in the flesh, he feels the patient great pain but not very severe.
et s’il est en la toile, si sent dolor forsenee.	and if it is in the net, he feels great pain extremely.
Et lors quant ceste cure desoit les mires, si covient que li malaides soit sovinez sus sa teste;	And when this treatment needs to take the fever down, it is advisable that the patient should be shaved above his head;
et puis seigne d’enche le leu ou li apostumes est, et puis chaufe le cautere qui est semblans au rais, de coi ci est li forme:	and then apply the poultice where the abscess is, and then heat the cautery which resembles an arrow, because this is the form:
Et cauterize I cautere tant que li keurs soit ars, et viegne jusc’a syphac, tant que li porreture soit toute fuers;	Instruct to cauterize as long as the keys are hot, until they come forth with pus, so that the infection is completely burned.
aprés la cure selonc la cure des essues tant qu’il soit sanez;	After the treatment as described, until he is well.
et ne covient mie que de cest cautere use nuls fuers que cil qui ait estudieit longement en l’art de medicine, et par cui mains cestes maladies ont corrut aucune fois.	And it is not suitable for this cauterization to be used on anyone except one who has studied for a long time in the art of medicine, and whose hands have been able to cure these diseases at least once.
Adonques puet il hardiement ovrer, et toutevoies il me semble que mues vaut li laissier.	So it can be done with great courage, and I must say that it seems to me to be worth leaving.
dou cautere de pleuresin	How to cut the pericardium
Li ancien dirent que on doit faire a pleuresin cauteres de racines d’aristologe, et en teil maniere:	The old ones said to make the cauterization of the spleen with the roots of the aristolchic herb, in this way:
pren une racine d’aristologe longe, la plus grant que tu poras troveir, et soit seche, et soit ausi grosse et ausi longe comme tes dois;	Take a long root of aristolchic herb, as large as you can find, and make it dry, just as large and as long as your two fingers.
et la moille en oile, et l’emprens au feu, et cauterize I cautere entre la forcele et lou col, et II petis cauteres un poc en dessendant en la partie qui est desoz la barbe;	and the mold in oil, and grasp it with fire, and cauterize between the flesh and the neck, and two points are cauterized a little in descending to the area that is under the beard;
et II cauteres entre la quinte coste et la sisime, en declinant derrier un poc;	and two cauterize between the fifth rib and the sixth, at an angle a little after;
et I cautere emmi le pis, et I autre sus l’estomac, et I entre II espaules, et II as II costez dou pis defuers le cautere qui est entre II espaules;	one cauterize between the belly and the pubic bone, and one above the stomach, and two between the shoulders, and between the two ribs where the cauterization is between the shoulders;
et ne presser mie ta main, ains fai apertement ausi com en odorant.	and do not press my hand, but rather make an aperture so as to smell.
Et dirent aucun ancien que aucun home usent de cautere de feir semblant a I raseur, et l’eschaufent et le mettent entre les costes, tant qu’il vient a cel aposteme;	And an old man said that no one uses the fire cautery similar to this razor, and they put it between the ribs, until it comes to that abscess;
et saut fuers li dolor, si com nos avons dit en l’aposteme dou foie.	and let him burn with fire, as we have said in the passage of the liver.
Mais en cestui ovraige est paour ou li malaides muert maintenant, ou fistule i vient qui ne puet estre sanee.	But in this work there is fear for the sick now, or a fistula appears that cannot be cured.
de la mice	of the mouse.
Quant tu cures la maladie de la mice de ceu que nos avons dit as divisions des cures, et il ne profite mie, adonques i afierent III manieres de cautere que tuit sont boin.	When you treat the sickness of the mouse, as we have said about divisions of cures, and it does not profit, then they say there are three ways of cauterization that all are good.
Desquelz li une maniere si est que tu faices III cauteres, ou IIII, en lignant selonc la longor de la mice, selonc la figure dou cautere dou foie que nos avons dit devant;	From which some say that you should do three cauterizations, or four, binding as the length of the mouse, according to the figure of the liver cautery that we have said before.
et n’apresser mie ta main a tout le cautere, et soit li malaides sovins sor son dos;	and do not hurry your hand with the cautery, and let the patient sit on his back;

et lieve le keur qui est endroit la mice, ou li coutes dou malaide vient devers senestre, et soit li elevations dont tu lieves le keur selonc la keur, selonc la longesce dou cors, et li cautere soient selonc la largesce dou cors.	and lift the wound that is directed to the mouse, or when the cut on the malady comes towards the left side, and let the elevations be lifted according to the wound, according to the length of the body, and the cautery should be according to the width of the body.
Aprés i boute les II ners enflamez tant que li keurs soit perciez de l’autre part, et puis trai fuers le cautere, et ensi en i avra IIII.	After they have applied the second ointment, you should burn the fire cautery until it is perceived by the other side, and then take out the fire, and so in this manner there will be four.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize a tot le cautere a III ners.	But if you see, if all the cautery has burned with two ointments.
Aprés le cure quant il a geteit porriture par lonc tens, et ce vaut mues que li autre des cures devant dites.	After the wound has gotten putrid due to long time, and this is an excuse that the other treatments before mentioned.
de ydropisie	From dropsy, instruct the patient to let the hairs grow long and even; and if they prick at their base, hold the eyes steady so they do not move until they grow.
Cautere ne vaut a ydropique, fors c’a la maniere qui est apelee «asclytes».	Cautery does not apply to dropsy, except when done in the way called "asclytes".
Quant tu la cures selonc les manieres que nos avons dit en divisions, et ta cure ne profite mie, adonques covient il que tu li faices IIII cauteres entor la boude, et I sus l’estomac, et un sus le foie, et I sus la mice, et II derrier le dos sus l’espinee, et I endroit le pis;	When you cure according to the manners we have told in divisions, and your treatment does not benefit, then it is necessary that you make four cauteries inside the wound, and one on the stomach, one on the liver, and one on the spleen, and two behind the back on the spine, and one towards the belly.
et soit li cauteres bien pres de l’espés dou keur.	and let the cauteries be very close to the spine of the cut.
Aprés laisse le cautere aovert por giter porriture lonc tens, et ne lassier mie la cure dou malaide aprés le cautere;	After let the cautery to close for a long time, and do not leave the patient's cure after the cautery;
et sanation se hasterait, et seront ensamble les II ententions avec l’aide de Deu.	and healing would come quickly, and both wounds will unite with God's aid.
Li forme dou cautere por le ventre soit li clavile que nos avons devant mostreit;	the form of the cautery for the abdomen is as we have shown before;
et cil por le dos soit olivaire, selonc ceu qu’il est ci devant mis.	and that for the back should be olive oil, according to what it is put there previously.
de l’enfleure des piez	of the swelling of the bones
Quant li piez sont enflez a celui qui est ydropique, et sont plain d’awe citrine, il covient que tu cauterizes sus le dos dou piet entre l’auriculaire et l’anulaire;	When the feet are swollen in one who is dropical and filled with a yellow pus, it is necessary to cauterize on the back of the foot between the little toe and the ring finger;
et lieve ta main avec le cautere sens torner.	and lift your hand with the cautery as it turns.
Et n’entrer mie trop em parfont, ensi sarrait fuers li awe citrine, et soit li cauteres selonc cest forme:	And do not enter too deeply, for so would the fire burn the citrine, and thus the cautery should be done in this form:
Aprés fai sus II jambes II cauteres en chescune jambe a la pointe dou cutellaire;	After do this, make two cauterizations on each foot at the tip of the cutlass.
et soit li cauteres dou lonc, l’un desoz le genoil devant et l’autre defuers, enmi la jambe;	And so let the fire cautery be performed on the long one, with one below the knee in front and the other behind it, on the leg;
et laisse les cauteres aovers longement sens curer, que li awe en isse;	and let the cautery be left open for a long time to cure what is inside;
aprés le cure des autres cures que nos avons dit.	after the other treatments that we have mentioned.
de la menoison	of the illness
Quant solution de ventre vient de froidor et de moistor, tant que li vertus retentive et digestive qui est ou stomac et en l’intestine est afleboie, et ne puet estre curez par manieres de cures;	When a stomach ailment comes from cold and moisture, such that the virtues retained and digestives which are in the stomach and intestines are thrown off, and cannot be cured with any other treatments;
et tu vois le malaide bien soffrant et de fort vertut, si fai I grant cautere sus l’estomac selonc ceu qu’il en a parleit ci devant ou cautere de l’estomac, au cautere circule;	and you see the patient suffering greatly and with great virtue, so do on him the cautery of the stomach as he has spoken about it before or the stomach cautery which we have mentioned before, the cautery that circles;
et IIII cauteres entor la boude subtilz a tout I cautere clavile subtil, et II cauteres sus les hainches.	And the fourth cautery is performed on the subtle veins under all cauteries with a needle very fine, and two cauteries are done above the haunches.
Et se tu vois les moistors habundans et le malaide soffrant, se li fai cautere sus le poignil, et I cautere sus chaicun yle, et II petis cauteres sus l’estomac delez le grant, car li cure est profitans quant il i a bone aide.	If you see moistures abundant and the patient suffering, then make fire cautery on the navel, and fire cautery on each joint, and twice make fire cautery on the stomach near the great one, because the cure is beneficial when it has good help.
de la cure des emorroydes	Of the treatment of hemorrhoids.
Quant les emorroydes sont ou fondement, ou une ou plusors, et sont ancienes et sont de grosses humors froides et moistes corrumpues, et sont curees si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie, si fai cauteres:	When the hemorrhoids are located at the base, or one, and more, and are old and consist of large cold and moist humors corrupted, and are treated as we have said in sections, but it does not benefit, perform cauteries:
III sus l’espine dou dos, celi qui est tout defuers desoz almecdate poc et poc en triangulant, et I cautere desoz la boude II dois;	Three above the spine on the back, those who are behind the almeda to and fro in a triangular manner, and one cautery below the vein two.
et se tu penses que ses estomac soit refroidiez, et li viande ne cuise, et on voit enfler la faice, adonques li faice on I grant cautere sus le stomac, si com il est devant dit, et I autre sus le foie, et I autre sus la mice a tout le cautere clavile;	and if you think that his stomach is cold, and the meat does not cook, and it swells in the face, then give one cautery on the stomach, as has been said, and one above the liver, and one above the spleen with all fine needles.
et laisse le cautere overt lonc tens.	and let the fire cautery remain for a long time.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	After the treatment the limb must be allowed to recover.
de la charnositeit qui est nommee «thelul»	from the fat which is called "thelel
Quant tu copes althelul, si eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et puis le met tout embraseit sus cel althelul copeit;	When you cut with the knife, if it seems to be frozen like a scythe, and then sets everything on fire that was cut.
et i laisse tant ta main que li cauteres viegne a la naissance de la voine, de coi li sans cort;	and let it rest as long as the cautery comes to life at the opening of the vein, so that there is no wound.
fai ceu une fois ou II, et s’il i a mout d’althelul, si cauterize chaicun si com nos avons dit;	do this once or twice, and if there is much of the cut, cauterize each one as we have said.
aprés les cure d’oignemens profitans tant qu’il soient sanez;	after applying ointments for a profit as long as they are healing.
et se tu cauterizes d’un cautere grant sus alchatim, si avra plus grant aide.	and if you cauterize with a great fire on the affected area, it will have more aid.
de plaie mal curee	of badly treated wounds
Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere.	When the patient cannot endure torture or opening, we will tell him in his own words, if he comes to this illness that cannot be healed except by cautery.
Quant a aucun vient fistule, et est enveillie et giete porriture et moistors corrumpues, si la doies prover a tot une tente subtil, et garde que tu saiches a tot la tente combien elle a de parfont.	When there is an ulcer, and it is old and covered with putrid pus and corrupted moisture, if you press to see whether the entire wound is tender, observe that you know how deep the wound is.
Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et le boute en la fistule selonc la quantiteit que li tente i est entrée, et rencomence lou cautere tant que cil cors porris et corrumpus soient ars, une fois, ou II ou III, selonc la quantiteit de som besoing;	After the cauterization which seems like a razor, and pour it into the fistula according to the quantity that is entered, and resume the cauterization until the flesh burns and corrupts once or twice, or three times, according to how much there is need.
et te warde d’ardre lé nerf qui sunt enqui, et des grans voinnes.	and guard the strong nerves that are strained, and the large veins.
se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans;	if the fistula goes to the body of the bladder and intestines, guard them well, and do not perform this fire on them unless they are in a walnut shell, and think they are not human.
aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez, et se li leus est saielez, et les matieres sont ostees lonc tens, adonc saiches que li leus est sanez entierement;	after treating the patient until they are healthy, and if the humors are imbalanced, and the materials are long-lying, then you should know that the patient is entirely healthy.
et se les matieres ne sont ostees, saiche que li leus est troez, et corrumpus li os au font;	And if the materials are not bones, know that the lead is heavy, and corrupts the bone.
et ensi com un de ces que nos dirons en son leu.	and so as one of these which we will speak of in its place.
de la maladie des reins	Of kidney disease
Quant dolor de froit vient as rains, et de grosse ventositeit, et ne prent talant de femme, adonc covient il que tu li fais cautere sus les rains d’une part et d’autre au cautere clavile que nos avons devant dit;	When pain from a blow comes with great swelling and does not take effect in a woman, then it is fitting that you apply cautery on the swollen parts of one side and the other, as we have said about the cautery claw.
et se nos le cauterizons em mileu, si avra III cauteres en ligne, et se feront plus grant aide.	and if our cauteries touch an artery, then have three more cauteries in a line, and they will give greater aid.
de la vessie	From the vessel
Quant li vessie est mole et foible de froit et de moistor, si que li malaides retient l’urine, adonc li fai cautere en la partie defuers sus la vessie, la ou encomencent li poil dou poignil, et I a destre et I a senestre, et soit chescuns cauteres si lons com li nous d’un poce;	When the bladder is mole and weak from blows and moisture, if the patient retains urine, then make cautery in the part behind the bladder, where the hair of the nipple begins, on both the right and left side, each one making cauteries as long as they can with one stroke.
et li fais I cautere defuers le dos, ou II se tu en as besoing;	and he makes fire cautery on his back, or if he needs to do it there.
et soit li cauteres clavile selon la forme devant dite.	and let the fire cautery be cut like that.
de la marris	From the intestines
Quant li marrix est froide et moiste, et ne laisse mie por ceu a concevoir, et les flors sont corrumpues et lor termines tarde;	When the marrow is cold and moist, and does not conceive again, and the flesh is corrupted and its ends are late.
et quant elles vienent, si sent grant dolor:	and when they come, it causes great pain:
adonques covient il c’on li faice III cauteres entor la boude, si com nos avons dit ou cautere de la vessie, et II cauteres defuers le dos;	therefore it is fitting that one makes fire cautery around the mouth, as we have said, and fire cautery on his back;
et soit li cauteres clavile, si com nos avons dit.	and let him make fire cautery of the shoulder, as we have said.
de la hainche	of the shoulder
Quant les moistors viscouses dessendent a la boiste de la hainche, et por ceste cause si se muet de son leu, et li signes est que li cuisse est plus longe que li autre quant on le mesure ensamble;	When the swollen viscous substances flow from the boil of the gallbladder, and because of this he moves out of his place, and the signs are that the knee is longer than the other when measured together;
et est trovez li leus dou departement vuis, si covient que tu cauterizes le malaide sus la boiste de la hainche a I cautere semblant au cercle, et seigne devant le leu entor la boiste si com elle torne, si que li boiste soit dedens le cercle;	and when it is found that the joints are separated by this movement, so it is fitting to cauterize the patient over the thorn of the groin, in a cautery similar to a circle, and signifying before the joint as it turns, so that the thorn may be inside the circle;
et si soit li cauteres telz com cil dont on a cauterizeit le stomac.	and if the cauterizations are like those of the stomach that one has cauterized.
Et se cist cauteres ne t’est presens, se li fai III cauteres de l’olivaire grans, et soit li cauteres ausi parfont com tous li keurs;	And if this cauterization is not present, make three cauterizations of the olive tree oil, and apply them as thick as all the scars.
et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and treat the patient until he is healed.
de la dolor de la hainche	Of the pain of the groin
Quant dolor vient en la boiste de la hainche, et c’est de froidor et de moistor, et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en la division et li cure ne vaut, et li maladie est anciene:	When pain comes to the groin of the groin, and it is caused by cold and moisture, and the patient has been treated with what we have said in the section on division, but the treatment does not work, and the disease is old.
adonc covient il que tu purges le malaide des grosses humors de pilules fetides, ou autres pilules bones semblans.	Then it is necessary to purge the patient of great humors of old pills or other hard pills that resemble them.
Aprés li fai cautere;	After cutting (the hair)
et li maniere dou cautere si est selonc II manieres:	and the manner of cautery is according to two ways:
c’est a savoir ensamble medicines ardans, et cautere de feu.	which are to be assembled with medicines hot, and fire cautery.
Cautere de feu si est selonc mout de manieres, desquelz li uns est telz:	Fire cautery is according to many ways, of which some are such that:
que tu cauterize sus la boiste de la hainche III cauteres triangulalz selonc ceste forme, et i fai bone profunditeit et grant, et ait entre chaicun cautere d’espaice la groissece d’un doi, et soit li cauteres olivaire;	that you cauterize on the flesh of the cheek three fire cauteries according to this shape, and make a strong and deep wound, and put between each cautery the space equal to the thickness of two doves, so that the cauteries are olive-shaped.
aucune fois fait on cautere en mileu sus lou chief de la hainche, por coi il en i a IIII selonc ceste forme:	Never is cautery performed in the middle of the cheek bone because there are four corresponding wounds according to this form:
Et se tu vues, si le cauterize au cautere dou cercle que nos avons devant dit en la dislocation de la hainche;	And if you see, when the cut is made by the cautery of a circle as we have described in the dislocation of the cheek bone;
mais fai en teil maniere que li cercles conteigne toute la hainche, et tous li espés dou keur soit ars.	but make it in such a way that the circle contains all of the cheek bone, and all the thick parts of the wound are seared.
Et c’est li maniere c’on fait en sciatique, quant li dolor tient en la hainche, et ne parvient mie jusc’a la cuisse ne jusc’a la jambe.	And this is the way it is done in sciatique, when the pain holds in the gout, and does not come to just below the knee or just below the leg.
Et s’ele vient jusc’a la cuisse et la jambe, se li fai II cauteres lai ou li malaides dit que li dolor li tient, et I cautere desus la cheville IIII dois, a la partie senestre un poc;	And if it comes just to the thigh and knee, then make two cauteries there, where the patient says that the pain lies, and four cauteries above the ankle, to the left side by one thumb.
et soit li cauteres cutellaire, et soit arse li espesseté dou keur;	and let the cauteries be made with a cutting instrument, and sear the thick parts of the wound.
et se li malaides sent que li dolor s’estende jusc’a dois dou piet ou pres d’enqui, se le cauterize la ou il sent la dolor III poins ou IIII au cautere qui est apelez «poins».	and if the patient feels that the pain spreads to two or three feet from the spot where it is felt in the cautery, and he is pricked at the place where the pain is felt for three points or four points, which is called "points".
Et se mestiers est, se li en fai plus;	And if it is thus, that he makes more.
et se il seit que li dolor soit desoz le genoil vers la cuisse, se li fais cautere au cautere cutellaire ou circulaire, et te done bien garde en tous tes cauteres que tu n’i lassier mie tant le cautere que tu brules les ners et les grans arteres, et que tu ne faices au malaide plus grant nuisance et contraction.	and if it is so that the pain is below the knee towards the thigh, then he cuts at the cutlery or circular cautery; and take good care in all your cauteries that you do not cauterize too much, lest you burn the nerves and great arteries, and cause more annoyance and contraction to the patient.
Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez.	And I myself have seen others who had fire cautery on the ankle of the foot, and let them burn so that the leg was completely severed, and also the toes, and they became recognized and corrupted all the toes.
Aprés une solution de ventre dont il ot la mort.	After a belly solution that killed him.
Et se li dolors est en II parties ensamble, fai cautere en l’une et en l’autre, selonc ceste maniere.	And if the pain is in both parts together, perform fire cautery on one and the other, according to this manner.
Et li saige dirent en la cautere de la hainche, de coi ci est li maniere, fai I tel fer et soit au chief ausi gros com uns nauvillon de dacte, ou un poc moins, et soit par entrechetres et soit des l’un entrechetres jusc’a l’autre d’espaice la quantiteit d’un nou de poce;	And the wise men say in the cautery of the hawthorn, for this is the manner: make a cut thus, with a blade one size smaller than a nail, or one point less; and cut alternately between two points, spaced apart like the length of a coin.
et soient li entrechetres aovers de II pars, et soient aussi comme noez, et i ait I mainche de fer bien fait;	and the fingers intertwined of two parts, and are also like those we have, and there is one iron band very well made;
et c’est li forme:	and this is the form:
Et soit eschaufez tant qu’il soit toz rouges et giete senteles, et puis le mette on sus la boiste de la hainche malaide, et soit tornez sus lou sain costeit;	And then it is heated until it is completely red and sends out smell, and then put it on the patient's groin, and turn it over to his healthy side;
et lou cauterize une fois I cautere reont et lou laisse III jors;	and after the cautery once is performed, and he lets the patient remain for three days;
et puis fai emplaustre de burre, et laisse la plaie aoverte lonc tens;	and then make plaster of butter, and let the wound be covered for long time;
aprés la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	after the treatment with binding until it is healed.
Albucasim dit que nos usons poc de cest cautere por la paor de son regart, et se voions poc qui en usent;	Alboçsim says that we should use little of this cautery because of the fear of its sting, and few people do so.
et toutevoie ceu est des boins cauteres, qui le puet soffrir, et lai ou il s’afiert.	and it is good to apply this, which he can endure, and at which place he will suffer.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi;	The cautery of medicine burns if you make an instrument between the cheeks, in which it lies on the edge of the mouth, and is made of iron or wood, for a long time, with two hooks, and has two parts, one between each.
et soient overt defuer et desus, et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:	And are joined together and on top, and assemble according to this form:
Aprés met sus la boiste de la hainche au malaide gisant sor suin costeit sain, et apresse ta main mout sus la boiste de la hainche;	After putting the hawthorn bandage on the patient lying on his side, and press your hand very hard on the hawthorn bandage;
aprés giete entre les II cercles de l’awe chaude qui soit chaufee au feu I poc, et li laisse une houre dou tens, et soffre li malaides la chalor et l’arsure de li.	After putting between the two circles of hot wax which is heated in a pot, and letting it sit for one hour with ten, and suffer the patient the heat and the inflammation.
Car il i trueve mordication ausi com de feu;	It is found to have a bite like of fire;
et quant li mordications iert passee, se lieve ta main avec l’estrument et leve la hainche d’awe douce, et laisse ensi III jors, et met sus burre tant que ceu qui est noir de l’eschaudure soit osteit;	and when the mordication has passed, lift your hand with the instrument and raise the heel of a sweet herb, and let it be so for three days, and put on butter until what is black from the ash falls out;
et lou laisse III jors que porriture en istrait;	and let him sit for three days that fermentation may be extracted;
et ceu serait li derriene aide aprés le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	And what would be the rear part aid after the treatment of wounds, until he is healed.
Et se li dolor s’est estendue jusc’a la cuisse ou jusc’a la jambe, se li fai I estrument que teigne awe selonc ceu que tu as fait en la hainche igaument;	And if the pain has extended just to the thigh or just to the leg, make the same instrument that you have made before in a larger way;
et c’est li maniere de l’awe chaude, et je l’ai escripte ou traitier de la rectification de medicine.	and this is the manner of the sweet herb, and I have written it in the treatment of medical correction.
Pren alcali et chaulz vive, autant de l’une com de l’autre, et les broie ensamble, et les met en I nuef pot.	Take quicklime and live sulfur, equal amounts of each, grind them together, and put them in a new pot.
ou il ait I petit pertuis defuer se que li pointe d’un raisor i puisse entreir;	If there is a small opening, do not open it so that the point of an arrow can enter.
et met desor celui pot I autre pot bien plombeit, et met sus alcali et chalz et awe douce sus, tant qu’il en i ait I doi desus les poudres cant tu l’avras bien preingte a ta main;	And put the other pot into a good place, and fill it with plumb, and place ash and chalk on top, and pour honey over them, until there are two powder residues left; thus you will have taken it well in your hand.
et le laisse ensi tant qu’il en dessende awe ague et chiece ou pot plombeit, puis pren toute cele awe, et la giete sus chalz et sus alcali si com devant.	And let it remain in that state until the powder comes down ash and cinder or into the pot with plumb, then take all of that, and place it on chalk and ash as before.
Et lors si sera mout ague et est aministree en mou d’ovraiges de medicine et en cauteres d’autres membres.	And when it is very hot and has been administered in the manner of overages of medicine and by cauterys of other members.
Car elle fait auteil oevre com feus, et si a autres medicines dont on cauterize bien la hainche ensi com tesisie et miel anacardi et chalz avec savon, toutes ces choses mellees ensamble.	For it makes all other works like fire, and so also with other medicines; because when you cauterize well the navel as such, honey and acacia and almonds with lye, all these things mingled together make a mixture.
Et Galiens nos raconte une cure dont uns hons fut curez de la dolor de la hainche et de la voine sciatique, et lou loe mout, et dit que on n’i fist autre cure, et qu’il en fut sanez a une soule fois quant on ot fait ceste cure, et il se fut baigniez si com il l’enseigne ci aprés.	And the Greeks tell us of a cure that one man was cured of the pain of his vein and sciatic nerve, and he spoke highly of it, and said that no other cure is needed, and he became sane for only once when this cure was performed, and he took a bath as he taught later on.
Et dist en teil maniere que tu preignes dou litargire vert fres et sec, et le broie mout avec I poc de graisse, et met sus la hainche et sus la cuisse et sus la jambe ou la dolor tient, et la lie;	And instruct him in this manner to press with the lard green and fresh and dry, and grind it much with a little fat, and put on the groin and on the thigh and on the leg where the pain lies, and tie;
et li laisse III houres et par la quantiteit que li malaides ne sente plus l’arsure.	and let him leave for three hours and by the quantity that the patient feels no more pain.
Et puis le fai entrer ou bain tant que li cors li soit un poc arousez, et lou fai entrer ou lit, et li dolor s’en ira toute et sera sanez.	And then put him into the bath so that his body may be slightly loosened, and put him to bed, and the pain will go away completely and he will be cured.
Et saiches que nuls ne doit user de cautere de telz medicines, se ceu n’est aprés l’evacuation de cors.	And know that no one should use fire cautery of such medicines, unless they are after the evacuation of the body.
Et Dyascorides dist que quant li voine sciatique est cauterizee de fiens de chievre, si i aide mout;	And Dioscorides says that when the sciatic vein is cauterized with horse's tendon, if it does help;
et doit estre fais li cauteres en teil maniere.	and must be done in this manner.
Prenez lainne et la beurez d’oile vielz, et metez sus la fossete qui est entre le pouce dou piez et l’autre qui est apelez foscile.	Take linen and anoint it with old oil, and put it on the fossa that is between the little toe and the other one called the foscile.
Aprés pren fiens de chievre sec, et l’empren a feu tant qu’il soit charbons, et lou met sus la laine, et le laisse tant qu’il soit estains;	After taking dried horse's tendon, and applying it to the fire until it is carbonized, then putting it on wool and letting it soak in that.
et refai encor ensi, et ne cesser de faire ensi tant que tu penses par sens qu’il viegne jusc’a la hainche, et que li dolor soit cessee;	And redo again thus, and do not cease to do so until you think with your mind that it will come just to the shoulder joint, and that the pain will be ceased;
et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».	and this manner of cautery is called "cautery of cheese".
de la dolor dou dos	of the pain of the back
Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.	When pain comes to the back, whether by falling or by percussion, or by excessive evacuation, or because of swelling of cold matter, none of these things is worth cautery, except for those who come from an infusion of cold matter.
Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne V cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir;	it is fitting that after this, the patient should be void of fetid pills or other similar things; and on his back, in such place as where the pain lies, three signs made of fire, one for each line, and in each line cautery or more according to virtue and quantity that the patient can bear;
et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»;	and it shall be made the cautery according to the cautery which is called "pains";
et se tu vues, fai III cauteres ou IIII au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:	and if you see, make three cauteries or four at the jointed claw cauterizing according to this form:
Maintes fois vient ceste maladie as petis enfans, et li signes de l’encomencement si est qu’il ont estroite alainne quant il se lievent, et paor;	This illness comes many times to small children, and the signs of its beginning are that they have a crooked arm when it starts to move, and fear.
et tu trueves en la derriene espinee dou dos et en nous l’apparance qui vient sus les autres espinees.	And you will find in the lower spine of the back and in the appearance that comes with the other spines.
Quant tu vois ceu et tu le vues curer, si le cauterize au cautere de celcle selonc ceste forme.	When you see this and observe how to cure it, cut off the affected area according to this form.
Si que li cautere porpreigne chescune partie de l’espinee egaument.	If you prick with cauterization each part of the spine increasingly.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize entor l’espinee au cautere poignant II lignes ou III, et soient li poins pres l’uns de l’autre.	And if you see, if you cut into the spine at a point just behind the second vertebra, or the third, and the points are close together.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez selonc ceu que nos avons dit, et warde que tu n’amenistrer cautere en gilbositeit qui soit en spame de nerf.	After the cure, keep the patient until he is healthy as we have said, and be careful not to apply cauterization to areas of swellings or inflammation which are in the grasp of a nerve.
de la dolor des jointes	Of the pain of joints
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere:	When pain is in joints due to moisture that are spread out in each body member, and when pain comes in the feet, which they call "podagre" properly, and when it is caused by cold reasons and medicines cannot cure it, even then are cured by cautery in this manner:
fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	make a fire of cautery around the joint in the foot, and use olive oil according to this form:
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	And if there is pain where you press on the face of the foot, do cautery to the entire point that we claim.
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire;	And if the pains come to both knees and other joints, and this happens often, for each knee or four of each part, the fire cautery is applied on each joint three times or four on each part, all over the olive treatment.
et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	and if you have a task of more weight, then do more, but keep your hand warm only until the fat part is frozen.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	And if the pains descend just to the groin and the back, instruct the patient to apply the fire cautery that we have discussed in his chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes;	And if pains are in the hands, so apply pain into the fold two lines.
et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main;	and if there is still no pain after, then apply pain to each joint and to the hair of the hand.
et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	and if pains come to both shoulders or both elbows, then apply fire cautery to each part, and do good governance for the patient, and administer remedies.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	But if you make good governance and purge the swelling, he will be made whole by God's help.
de la routure dou syfac	From the operation of the scalp
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor;	When rupture comes to flesh, and the swellings descend into wounds and it's new, then it is fitting that while you are treating the wound, do not let it be wounded again.
et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre;	and that they use things that clear the stomach, so that the pus descends from its belly;
aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors;	after which you seat him on his back between your hands, and he commands that he tightens his leg as long as the swellings are healing, and you pull it to your hands, and he signs for you to cut over the rupture onto the bone of the elbow, and so make a mark like half of a circle above the body.
puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	then you inflate the cautery with what is its form:
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	Until he is white and his senses are clear.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu;	Let them remove the bowels to their place.
et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier;	and hold the fingers of the hands against which they do not return.
et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains;	and sew well the knees of the patient, and put a gauze over the wound in the flesh, and another one over the hand that holds the fingers.
puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os;	then put the cautery on the sign of the wrist until you reach the bone; and if you do not reach it at once, if it recurs again another time until you reach the bone.
et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere;	and beware carefully that the bile does not escape when you do the cautery.
que tu ne le brulasses;	so as not to burn it.
et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	and so let the patients not die from this.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	And instructs you to know that when you do not come close enough to the bone with the cautery, your work is worthless.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure;	And it is necessary that the cauterization of children be subtle according to their measure, and of adults also great according to their measure;
aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee;	after three days' treatment, take away the cauterized wound with butter until it is healed.
aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee;	after the patient has recovered from other treatments until he is fully healed, and lay the sick person on their back for forty days, so that the wound may be well-healed.
et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	and it is necessary that their menstrual periods be slow to dry up, so that the bowels do not burst when they are going to move in the chambers.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors;	And after forty days, when he wishes to rise, dress him in a well-made bandage and bind it for another forty days;
et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire;	And give a good rest, so he works little and guards himself from excessive drinking and eating, and from drinking too high.
et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	and when he follows this teaching so is made completely whole.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	And I will say this after his treatment in his chapter.
de la routure dou ventre	of the operation on the abdomen.
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur;	When wounds come back in other places and are recognized, and you see that they do not grow again, if you apply cauterization according to its size, then take out one-third of the cure.
aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit;	after the treatment as we have said;
et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	and none of the ancients has said that you should cauterize with the fire at three angles according to this shape:
mais signe premier le leu d’enche et fai une ligne per la largesce desus la routure, et une autre defuers, et main ta main emmi a tout le cautere clavile.	but first mark the left side of the wound and make a line for its width, and another one afterwards, and tie your thumb tightly around the entire cauterization.
Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.	But the first cauterizations are lighter and more gentle.
de dolor anciene en aucun membre	Of olden pain in any member
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	When pain comes to any member, whether from a fall or from injuring it, and the pain lasts for a long time, and medicine cures are not effective, then it is necessary to be cauterized with the cautery called "poins", and to be cauterized according to the length of the member and its smallness and weakness and its virtue and its location of twisting and of its pain.
s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien;	if he is well after the first cauterization, it is good.
se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.	When the head of the shoulder is dislocated due to moisture, and it is reset but cannot stay in place, repeatedly dislocating with slight movement as we have experienced, then you must first reset the dislocation. Dislocations occur when a joint moves out of its place, which prevents it from moving, and the limb is misaligned, causing the patient great pain and injury.
de meselerie	Of clumsiness
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	The trouble is treated with no success by cauterization for great help, and the same illness that comes from the rotting of pus and melancholy.
Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief:	You can view cauterizer, take care that if the patient is at the beginning, and if he is cured according to what we have said in the division, and do not cut or stop moving, and you doubt that corruption seeps into the entire patient, then make cauterizers on the head:
I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous;	i have removed the hair from the head, and on the other side of the forehead to the end of the eyebrows;
et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel;	and one above the two horns, and one behind on the heel;
et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir;	and I leave your hand in such a way that the cautery comes to life just before the bone, and so much so that the scales come out strongly, so that the vapors of the large humors can come out.
et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.	and cut on the mouse according to what it is in front.
Et se li meselerie est partout esparse;	And if there is a separation everywhere;
et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et I cautere en som lou neis, et II cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et VI cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et I grant sus la crupie et I autre delez, et II sus les II espaules;	and it is clearly visible, so it is wise to use one of the cauterization techniques that we have mentioned earlier, and 1 cauters on the neck, and 2 in the throat area, and 6 on the spine at the back, and 1 on the groin and the other 1 on the lower back, and 2 on the shoulder blades.
et II sus les coutes, et II sus les tendrons dou pis, et I sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains;	and 2 on the sides, and 2 on the tendons of the leg, and 1 on each joint of the hands and feet, and on the depressions of the hands;
et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler;	and beware of the nails that are on top of the dead man's thigh, lest you burn them.
et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et I autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et I autre sus lou foie.	and at no time should the cautery be made on the bone of the finger joint, and another on the bone of the stomach, and another on the liver.
Et saiches que quant plus i fais de cautere, plus li fais d’aide, et mues li profite;	And know that when you do more cautery, the patient will gain more aid and benefit.
et saiches que li malaides ne sent point de dolor au cautere si com li sain le sentent, por ce que li cors est ja toz corrumpus.	and know that the sick do not feel pain from cautery at all, just as they feel it when they are healthy, because the body is already completely corrupted.
Et covient ke li cautere soient grant et petit selonc les membres et les jointures, selonc ceu que vos lou troverez en manieres des fers.	And it is fitting that the fire cautery should be large or small depending on the member and joints, as you will find in various iron tools.
Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	After treatment, wash the patient with flour and honey several times until they are healthy.
Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre;	When an inflammation comes to any member and is cured with medicines, oils, and plasters, but the patient does not recover, then you should do cautery on the member according to its size and shape.
et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur;	and so let the cauterizers take a little of the flesh where it is red.
puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	then the treatment for pains such as this until they are cured.
Et aucune fois fait on cautere et a la main et au piet et au dos, a l’issue dou nerf que muet le membre, et ensi si est ostee li enfleure;	And no one is cauterized by hand and foot and back until the nerve is muted and the limb becomes stiff.
et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors.	and no one interferes with this if it is not known by one who understands the members and the movements of the nerves.
de albaras	De albaras translates to "of wounds".
Quant li maladie qui est apelee «albaras» est enveillie, et li engien de medicine n’i valent rien, adonques le cauterize d’un cautere un poc parfont, selonc la quantiteit de l’espés dou keur, tant que li blenchour soit ostee, et soit muee sa color;	When the illness called "albaras" is old and worn out, and medicine does not help, then cauterize with a cautery, taking a little of the flesh to the depth of the redness, so much that the blanching comes out, and the color fades.
puis le cure de farine de veces et de lentilles avec oile roset et foilles de plantain, et sanc de colon et sanc d’alondre, de chescun une partie;	then the doctor gives them a mixture of flour from wheat and lentils with rose oil and leaves of plantain, and blood from a colt and blood from an alder tree, one part from each;
et soit mellez tout ensamble, et soit liiez d’un drapel, et soit aers au leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	and let everything be mixed together, and tie it with a cloth, and apply to the patient until they are healed.
li cure de chancre par cautere	the cure of cancrer by cautery
Quant chancre vient au comencement, et tu lou vues arrester, si le cauterize au cautere qui semble I cercle, tout entor au tour dou chancre.	When cancrer comes at the beginning, and you look to stop it, then cut with cautery on the cautery that seems to be around the entire circle of the cancrer.
Et toutevoie li saige dirent que on faice cautere ausi au mileu dou chancre;	And all the wise men say that one should also apply fire cautery to the middle of a wound.
et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois;	and all the wise men do not seem good to me, because I fear that it will cause ulceration and corruption, and I have never been able to bring this about.
et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres.	and the most troublesome thing is that they are cauterized inwards, with the cauterization called "circle", just as we have said of other cauterizations.
de l’enfleure qui ne puet meurer	of an edema that cannot die
Quant aucuns ait une maladie qui est apelee «adubelati», et elle tarde de meurer ou por la superfluiteit qu’ele fait ou por l’eaige dou malaide quant il est decrepites (c’est a dire trop vielz) et il a poc de sanc, ou por lou tens;	When some have a disease called "adubelati", and it delays dying because of its overflow or the old age of the sick man when he is very weak, and he has little blood, or because his time.
et tu la vues haster de meurer:	and to see it hasten to die:
adonques le cauterize entor de mout de petis cauteres en poignant;	and therefore the cautery should be cut off with many small cauteries in pricking.
aprés le laisse ensi.	after which he is left so.
Car elle se hastera de meureir.	It will soon die.
Et se tu la vues percier a tout le cautere, si chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	And if you see it pierced all with the cautery, so that the cauterization is of this form:
Et met ta main en mileu de cele maladie qui est apellee «adubelati» tant que li cauteres ait perciet lou keur, et soit telz li cauteres que li malaides lou sente defuers en teil maniere que li cours de la porriture soit alegis.	And put your hand in the middle of that disease which is called "adubelati" until the cauterization has pierced the vein, and so that the cauterization is made with such precision that the patient feels pain before it happens in this manner, so that the course of the infection may be delayed.
Aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	After the treatment until he is perfectly recovered.
li cure dou feu par fer	the cautery by iron.
Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.	Another type of disease that is called "corrodens", and it is nothing other than a gangrene of the limb, because it corrupts the limbs in the same way as fire corrupts dry wood.
Se tu vois ceste maladie en leu qui puisse soffrir cautere ensamble feu, adonques eschaufe les cauteres clavile mout petit et grant, selonc ceu qu’il covient au leu ou li maladie est;	If you see this disease in a person who can suffer fire cautery together, then take small and large nails, as much as is needed to the person or according to the disease.
aprés le cauterize de toutes pars tant que tu erraiche toute la corruption, et nen remaigne rien de li, que tout ceu qui est corrumpus ne soit osteit.	after the cautery of all parts until you eradicate all the corruption, and nothing remains except that all that is corrupted be destroyed.
Et puis le laisse III jors, et met sus les leus cauterizez soffre broiet avec oile tant que les eschaudures dou feu soient ostees, et toute li corruption.	And then let him lie for three days, and put on the patient's cauterized wounds with a cloth soaked in oil until the scalds from the fire are destroyed, and all the corruption.
Aprés lou cure d’oignemens engendrans char.	After this remedy is done with generated splinters.
Et se tu vois aprés III jors que chars saine ne naisse, c’est boin;	And if you see after three days that a healthy child does not come out, it's good;
et se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere sus ceu qui est demoreit des leus corrumpus.	and if this does not happen, then resume the cautery on the one who has been left in a state of corruption.
Et ceste mengeson est aucune fois esteit curee de medicine ague en leu de cautere de feu;	And this remedy has never been cured with medicinal water instead of the cautery of fire.
mais toutevoie cautere de feu est de plus grant aide, et j’ai ja dit la cure de la medicine ague en la division:	but that all cauteries of fire are of greater aid, and I have already said the remedy of medicinal water in division.
pren la quant tu en as mestier.	take what you need.
des porrelz qui vienent as piez	of worms that come to the bones.
Mout de fois avient que as piez par defuers naist une maladie qui est apelee «clos» selonc nostre entencion, et est une grosse chose fautree qui blece lou piet.	Often it happens that at the bones due to weakness a disease is born which is called "closed" according to our intention, and it is a big thing that wounds the bone.
Et li cauteres de ceste maladie si est selonc II manieres.	And the fire cauteries of this disease are according to two manners.
C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	That is to say, cauterizing with fire, and cauterizing with hot water.
Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges;	Cautery of fire is that you heat the cautery hair like a goose feather, and let it be made of good iron to the measure that it can penetrate the nail in all parts, and have subtle margins;
aprés le met tout chaut sus lou clou, et torne ta main tot entor le clou tant qu’il viegne au font dou clou;	After the he made it all hot on the nail, and turned your hand around the nail so that it comes to its proper place;
et lou laisse ensi III jors tant qu’il encomence giter porriture;	and then lets him sit for three days until he begins to sweat out the pus;
puis li fai un emplaustre de malves savaiges broiies avec seil, et laisse l’emplaustre sus toute la nuit, et li clous cherra et sera desracinez de ses racines.	then he makes an poultice of fresh raspberries crushed with thread, and lets the poultice on the entire wound all night, and the splinter will fall out and be loosened from its roots.
Puis cure le leu d’oignement enjanrant char tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat the joint with application of heat until it is healthy.
Et s’il sont convertit par defuers lou cors, et maintes fois avient et en mains et em piez, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere d’aigue chaude;	And if they have converted to fever, and it often happens in the hands and feet, then you should apply cauterization with hot water.
et est en teil maniere:	and is done in this way:
pren une cainne d’arain ou de fer, ou une penne de vouteul, et met sus lou clou et l’althelul, c’est asavoir porrelz verrues;	take a thorn or iron nail, or a feather from a quail, and put it on the splinter and the flesh, that is to say, to press out warts;
et met la cainne sus si qu’ele porpreigne tout entor, puis i met un poc d’awe chaude, et retien bien ta main, et presse ta main en tornant si que li marge de la cainne viegne a la racine dou clou, et puisse trover l’aigue chaude voie parfonde jusc’a la racine;	Instruct the patient to put the tourniquet on so that it pricks all around; and then put a little of hot water on it, and hold your hand well, and press your hand as you turn so that the margin of the tourniquet comes to the root of the nail, and can find its way through deep into the root.
et soffre li malaides un poc la mordication de l’aigue chaude une houre;	and let the patient suffer a little from the heat of the water for an hour;
puis le laisse ensi, et il se derracinera tous a tout ses racines.	then let him go so that he will all bleed out to its roots.
Ensi fai un aprés autre, tant que tu esraiches toz ces qui sont au cors, puis les cure des oignemens qui engenrent char.	Instruct a doctor to do this after that one, until you have checked all those who are in the body, then cure the limbs that bind tightly.
li cure dou trembler	cure of shaking
Quant aucuns tremble de froidor de ners, ou de fievre quartaine ou d’autre, si covient que tu li faices IIII cauteres ou IV sus l’espinee dou dos, I cautere entre chescune espinee;	When some are trembling from cold or from fever of the fourth kind, or from another disease, it is fitting that you make four cauteries or four on the spine of the back, and one cauterization between each spine.
et I cautere ou pez, et I sus l’estomac au cautere olivaire;	and take care of the foot, and apply the olive oil cautery to the stomach.
si laissera lou trembler, et se hastera li santez de la maladie froide.	if he will relax, and quickly recover from the disease of cold fever.
des pustules puans	of painless boils.
Aucune fois apperent par defuers le cors bathes, ou pustules puans, que vienent de grosses matieres corrumpues.	Never appear in its natural state the chest's boils or painless boils, which come from corrupted large matters.
si covient au premier quant eles apperent que on faice cautere sus chescun chief de la pustule:	if it is wise to cut first, when they appear that one does cauterize each head of the pustule:
un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.	a subtle cauterization with a fustel of myrtle wood, so that the point is gripped by fire, or with an aristoletum root, or with the lenticular cauterization.
Et aucune fois les cauterize on au comencement quant il aperent, selonc ceste maniere, et il ne puent croistre des enqui en avant, mais est desrompue li superfluitez dont il vienent, et sont sanez;	And at no time do cauterize it in the beginning when they appear this way, for according to this method, and they cannot increase or worsen beforehand, but the superfluities which come from it are ruptured, and healed.
mais il covient que ceu soit fait aprés l’evacuation de sanc.	But it is necessary to do this after the evacuation of blood.
quant li artere est copee	when an artery is cut.
Maintes fois avient grans decorremens de sanc de l’artere qui est copee a la plaie que vient au pardefuers, ou a l’incision de l’aposteme, ou au cautere dou membre, et as semblans choses;	Often happens great bleeding of the artery which is cut at the wound that comes to the surface, or in the incision of the abscess, or by fire cautery on the member, and similar things;
et est mout grief chose d’estenchier.	and is very pitiful to clean.
Et toutevoie quant ceu avient a aucun, si te haste de mettre ton doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne, et l’estrain mout tant que li sans soit apaisiez desoz ton doi, et que goute n’en isse plus;	And everyone sees that when this happens on anyone, if you hasten to put your two fingers on the wound of the vein, and press much so that there is no more blood, and the pain is not felt.
puis met au feu les cauteres olivaire plusors petis et grans tant qu’il soient tuit rouge;	then puts the olive oil cauteries, small and large, into the fire until they are all red.
puis empren I, ou grant ou petit selonc la plaie et lou leu en coi li artere est route, et met le cautere sus cele voine ou tu tiens ton doi, et tien le cautere tant sus que li sans soit restainchiez.	Instruct the patient to put on the cautery first, or a small one according to the wound and its location, and place the cautery on that vein where you hold your thumb, and keep it there until the bleeding is stopped.
Et s’il saut fuers quant tu lieves ton doi desus la voinne, et li cauteres estint, si pren hastivement I autre des cauteres qui sont au feu.	And if the fire jumps up when you lift your two fingers over the vein, and the cautery is extinguished, take haste and take another cautery that is on fire.
Et ne cesser de faire ceu l’un aprés l’autre tant que li sans soit estenchiez;	And do not stop doing this one after another, until the bleeding is stopped.
et warde que tu n’ardes lou nerf qui est delez, et que autre malice ne viegne sus lou malaide;	And beware that you do not burn the nerve near it, and that no other harm comes upon the patient.
et saiches que quant sans decourt de l’artere, c’on ne lou puet mie bien restenchier meismement quant li artere est grans, se ceu n’est par une des IIII manieres que nos avons dit:	And know that when the artery is not cut during the procedure, it cannot be properly closed itself because of the large artery. If so, this should be done by one of the four ways we have mentioned previously.
ou par cautere, ou par extraction quant ele n’est mie traite, ou par fort liement de fil, ou par medicines mises sus qui ont pooir de restenchier sanc;	or by cautery, or by extracting it when it is not treated, or by tying it tightly with thread, or by applying medicines that have the power to close the wound.
et soit liee et estrainte avennament.	And if bound and strained occurs.
Qui i amenistrera restenchement de liier estroitement de drapelz ou de metre choses ardans sus, ou autres semblans choses, se n’i profite se poc non.	Who will provide restening of a tightly bound member by covering it with bandages or putting hot things on top of it, or other similar things, unless there is no benefit.
Et se ce avient a aucun et il n’ait mie mire ne medicine present, si doit mettre son doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne si com nos avons dit, et bien estrendre tant qu’il soit restenchiez desus la plaie et desus la voinne;	And if this happens when he has no remedy or medicine present, then he must put his two fingers on the wound vein as we have said, and stretch it well so that it remains behind the wound and the vein.
et ne remuer lou doit, mais lou moille d’awe froide sovent que soit mout froide tant que li sans soit congelez et engrossiez et restenchiez;	and he must not move it, but let the moisture of the frosty cold water soak in, so that it becomes very cold, until it is frozen and thickened and remains behind.
et faice des enqui en avant ceu dont il a mestier de cauteres et de medicines.	and face the wound forward for those who need cauterization and medicine.
Ci encomence li secons livre des cures de taille	This begins the second book on the treatment of cuts.
Nos vos avons dit ou premier chapistre toute maladie en coi il covient cautere de feu, ou de medicine ardans, et les oquisons et les causes et les estrumens et les formes des cauteres;	As we have said in the first chapter, for every disease whether it requires cauterization with fire or with hot medicine, and the symptoms, causes, discharges, and forms of the cauterizations;
et ai mis celui chapistre des lou chief jusc’a piez, et je irai en cest chapistre par celi meisme voie por ceu c’on trueve plus legierement ceu c’on voura.	and I have placed that chapter of the surgery on the forehead just above the bone, and I will go into this same chapter by the same path because what is found there is more easily found than what we see.
Et ainsois que je encomence ceu, il covient, chier fil, que vos aprenez que en cest chapistre a plus de peril et de paor que ou premier des cauteres, et por ceu il covient plus grant cautele.	And so that I begin this work, it is necessary, dear son, that you learn that in this chapter there is more danger and fear than with the first cautery, and therefore it must be approached with greater caution.
Car en l’ovraige de cest chapistre avient maintes fois evacuation de sanc a l’ovrir la voinne, et a l’incision sus aposteme, et as cures des plaies, et a l’estraction des saiettes, et a l’incision sus la piere, et les semblans choses;	For in the work of this chapter, there is often the evacuation of blood when opening a vein, and incising an abscess, and in the treatment of wounds, and in the extraction of arrows, and in cutting into stones, and similar things; or it is doubt and fear, and many die.
ou il a doutance et paor, et en vient li mors a plusors.	where there is doubt and fear, and many die.
Et je vos amoneste que vos n’entreprenez folie.	And I warn you not to be foolish.
Car mout de manieres de gens vienent en cures.	For many kinds of people come in for treatment.
si vienent de telz qui s’aïrent si avec lor maladie qu’il muerent legierement por la forsenerie qu’il trueve de sa maladie, et de la grandour de son malice;	if they come from those who have been so affected by their illness that they die easily because of the strength of their suffering, and the great power of their malady;
et de ces doit on avoir paor.	and of these things one must have fear.
Et de ces i a qui te done son sens, et dit:	And as to what is said to you by this physician, and says:
«atendez, je sui garis»;	Wait, I am cured.
et li maladie est despitouse.	and the sickness is stubborn.
Il ne covient mie que vos vos consentez a ces qui vienent a vos qui ont ceste maniere, mais mettez plus grant cusanson en vostre honor qu’en vostre covoitise, et n’ovrez mie folement mais saigement de ceu dont vos estes certain, et dont vos poez avoir pris et los;	It is not fitting for you to only take advice from those who come to visit you in this manner, but rather put more consideration into your honor than into your covetousness, and do not be weak-hearted but wise about what you are certain of, and what you have acquired.
et usez de pronostication et de indication en cures de vos malaides a coi salus soit convertie;	and use prognosis and indication in the treatment of your sick patients to what end the salus (good health) is converted.
et ceu vos aidera a aquester bone renommee, et gloire, et memoire de loenge.	And this will help you gain a better reputation, and glory, and memory of praise.
Tres chier fil, Nostres Sires vos doint boin entendement et droiture, et se vos vuelle espireir de la sainte inspiration de sa main, amen.	Three most precious sons, our Lord gives you good understanding and right judgment, and if you wish to aspire to the holy inspiration of his hand, Amen.
Or je vos ai ordeneit cest chapistre en devisant par chapistres, selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre des cauteres, que je vos ai deviseit des le chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que vos trovez plus legierement ceu dont vos avrez mestier.	I shall translate the text line by line into English.
dou chief plein d’aigue	The chief full of water
Saiches que ceste maladie vient mout de fois as enfans a l’enfanter, et quant li baille estraint trop fort le chief de l’enfant;	It is observed that this disease comes often in children when the child strains too hard at the head.
et aucune fois vient ceu de cause reponue que on ne seit.	And sometimes it comes from a return that is not known.
Et je ne vis onques ceste maladie fuers qu’en enfans, et a toz ces que j’ai veus se hastait li mors;	And I have never seen this disease occur in adults, and all those that I have seen have had the mouth closed.
et por ceu me semble qu’il me vaut mues lassier l’ovraige en teilz cures.	And for this reason, I think it is worth wasting some time on treating the joint in several ways.
Et je vis I enfant de coi li chiés estoit plains d’aigue, et li chief engroissoit chescun jor tant qu’il ne lou pooit sostenir;	And I see that the child's knee was swollen with water, and every day its head would swell so much that it could no longer sustain.
et crut tant li moistor qu’il fut mors, et ceste moistor si est assemblee desoz l’os sus lou syphac, entre lou keur et l’os;	and he believed so much about moisture that it killed him, and this moisture is assembled beneath the bone above the spleen, between the kidney and the bone.
et li ovraiges si est telz se li moistor est entre lou keur et l’os, et li apostemes est petis, que tu fendes emmi lou chief une fendure large;	and the wounds are such that if moisture is between the kidney and the bone, and the abscess is small, you should make a wide incision in his chest.
et soit ausi longe com II nous, tant que li mostor corre;	and be as long as ours, so that the moisture runs out;
et vez ci la forme dou spatumile:	and cut it there in the shape of a spatula:
Se li moistor est plus creue, et li aposteme soit plus grans, si fai II fendures en maniere d’une croix, selonc ceste forme:	If the moisture is more deep, and the abscess is bigger, then you should make two incisions in the shape of a cross, according to this form:
